[]EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tif matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\t}\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil // Short-circuit: AND with nothing is nothing.\n\t}\n\n\t// The set of signatures for the right-hand side Vector.\n\trightSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\t// Add all rhs samples to a map so we can easily find matches later.\n\tfor _, sh := range rhsh {\n\t\trightSigs[sh.signature] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\t// If there's a matching entry in the right-hand side Vector, add the sample.\n\t\tif _, ok := rightSigs[lhsh[i].signature]; ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) VectorOr(lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany:\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\tcase len(lhs) == 0: // Short-circuit.\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, rhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\tcase len(rhs) == 0:\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\t}\n\n\tleftSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\t// Add everything from the left-hand-side Vector.\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tleftSigs[lhsh[i].signature] = struct{}{}\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t}\n\t// Add all right-hand side elements which have not been added from the left-hand side.\n\tfor j, rs := range rhs {\n\t\tif _, ok := leftSigs[rhsh[j].signature]; !ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, rs)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) VectorUnless(lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tif matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\t}\n\t// Short-circuit: empty rhs means we will return everything in lhs;\n\t// empty lhs means we will return empty - don't need to build a map.\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\t}\n\n\trightSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, sh := range rhsh {\n\t\trightSigs[sh.signature] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tif _, ok := rightSigs[lhsh[i].signature]; !ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\n// VectorBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Vectors, excluding set operators.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) VectorBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, returnBool bool, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper, pos posrange.PositionRange) (Vector, error) {\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"many-to-many only allowed for set operators\")\n\t}\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil // Short-circuit: nothing is going to match.\n\t}\n\n\t// The control flow below handles one-to-one or many-to-one matching.\n\t// For one-to-many, swap sidedness and account for the swap when calculating\n\t// values.\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\tlhs, rhs = rhs, lhs\n\t\tlhsh, rhsh = rhsh, lhsh\n\t}\n\n\t// All samples from the rhs hashed by the matching label/values.\n\tif enh.rightSigs == nil {\n\t\tenh.rightSigs = make(map[string]Sample, len(enh.Out))\n\t} else {\n\t\tfor k := range enh.rightSigs {\n\t\t\tdelete(enh.rightSigs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trightSigs := enh.rightSigs\n\n\t// Add all rhs samples to a map so we can easily find matches later.\n\tfor i, rs := range rhs {\n\t\tsig := rhsh[i].signature\n\t\t// The rhs is guaranteed to be the 'one' side. Having multiple samples\n\t\t// with the same signature means that the matching is many-to-many.\n\t\tif duplSample, found := rightSigs[sig]; found {\n\t\t\t// oneSide represents which side of the vector represents the 'one' in the many-to-one relationship.\n\t\t\toneSide := \"right\"\n\t\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\t\t\toneSide = \"left\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tmatchedLabels := rs.Metric.MatchLabels(matching.On, matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t\t// Many-to-many matching not allowed.\n\t\t\tev.errorf(\"found duplicate series for the match group %s on the %s hand-side of the operation: [%s, %s]\"+\n\t\t\t\t\";many-to-many matching not allowed: matching labels must be unique on one side\", matchedLabels.String(), oneSide, rs.Metric.String(), duplSample.Metric.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\trightSigs[sig] = rs\n\t}\n\n\t// Tracks the match-signature. For one-to-one operations the value is nil. For many-to-one\n\t// the value is a set of signatures to detect duplicated result elements.\n\tif enh.matchedSigs == nil {\n\t\tenh.matchedSigs = make(map[string]map[uint64]struct{}, len(rightSigs))\n\t} else {\n\t\tfor k := range enh.matchedSigs {\n\t\t\tdelete(enh.matchedSigs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tmatchedSigs := enh.matchedSigs\n\n\t// For all lhs samples find a respective rhs sample and perform\n\t// the binary operation.\n\tvar lastErr error\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tsig := lhsh[i].signature\n\n\t\trs, found := rightSigs[sig] // Look for a match in the rhs Vector.\n\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Account for potentially swapped sidedness.\n\t\tfl, fr := ls.F, rs.F\n\t\thl, hr := ls.H, rs.H\n\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\t\tfl, fr = fr, fl\n\t\t\thl, hr = hr, hl\n\t\t}\n\t\tfloatValue, histogramValue, keep, err := vectorElemBinop(op, fl, fr, hl, hr, pos)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlastErr = err\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase returnBool:\n\t\t\thistogramValue = nil\n\t\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue = 1.0\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue = 0.0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase !keep:\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric := resultMetric(ls.Metric, rs.Metric, op, matching, enh)\n\t\tif !ev.enableDelayedNameRemoval && returnBool {\n\t\t\tmetric = metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t}\n\t\tinsertedSigs, exists := matchedSigs[sig]\n\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToOne {\n\t\t\tif exists {\n\t\t\t\tev.errorf(\"multiple matches for labels: many-to-one matching must be explicit (group_left/group_right)\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tmatchedSigs[sig] = nil // Set existence to true.\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// In many-to-one matching the grouping labels have to ensure a unique metric\n\t\t\t// for the result Vector. Check whether those labels have already been added for\n\t\t\t// the same matching labels.\n\t\t\tinsertSig := metric.Hash()\n\n\t\t\tif !exists {\n\t\t\t\tinsertedSigs = map[uint64]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\tmatchedSigs[sig] = insertedSigs\n\t\t\t} else if _, duplicate := insertedSigs[insertSig]; duplicate {\n\t\t\t\tev.errorf(\"multiple matches for labels: grouping labels must ensure unique matches\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tinsertedSigs[insertSig] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, Sample{\n\t\t\tMetric:   metric,\n\t\t\tF:        floatValue,\n\t\t\tH:        histogramValue,\n\t\t\tDropName: returnBool,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out, lastErr\n}\n\nfunc signatureFunc(on bool, b []byte, names ...string) func(labels.Labels) string {\n\tif on {\n\t\tslices.Sort(names)\n\t\treturn func(lset labels.Labels) string {\n\t\t\treturn string(lset.BytesWithLabels(b, names...))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tnames = append([]string{labels.MetricName}, names...)\n\tslices.Sort(names)\n\treturn func(lset labels.Labels) string {\n\t\treturn string(lset.BytesWithoutLabels(b, names...))\n\t}\n}\n\n// resultMetric returns the metric for the given sample(s) based on the Vector\n// binary operation and the matching options.\nfunc resultMetric(lhs, rhs labels.Labels, op parser.ItemType, matching *parser.VectorMatching, enh *EvalNodeHelper) labels.Labels {\n\tif enh.resultMetric == nil {\n\t\tenh.resultMetric = make(map[string]labels.Labels, len(enh.Out))\n\t}\n\n\tenh.resetBuilder(lhs)\n\tbuf := bytes.NewBuffer(enh.lblResultBuf[:0])\n\tenh.lblBuf = lhs.Bytes(enh.lblBuf)\n\tbuf.Write(enh.lblBuf)\n\tenh.lblBuf = rhs.Bytes(enh.lblBuf)\n\tbuf.Write(enh.lblBuf)\n\tenh.lblResultBuf = buf.Bytes()\n\n\tif ret, ok := enh.resultMetric[string(enh.lblResultBuf)]; ok {\n\t\treturn ret\n\t}\n\tstr := string(enh.lblResultBuf)\n\n\tif changesMetricSchema(op) {\n\t\t// Setting empty Metadata causes the deletion of those if they exists.\n\t\tschema.Metadata{}.SetToLabels(enh.lb)\n\t}\n\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToOne {\n\t\tif matching.On {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Keep(matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Del(matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, ln := range matching.Include {\n\t\t// Included labels from the `group_x` modifier are taken from the \"one\"-side.\n\t\tif v := rhs.Get(ln); v != \"\" {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(ln, v)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Del(ln)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tret := enh.lb.Labels()\n\tenh.resultMetric[str] = ret\n\treturn ret\n}\n\n// VectorscalarBinop evaluates a binary operation between a Vector and a Scalar.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) VectorscalarBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs Vector, rhs Scalar, swap, returnBool bool, enh *EvalNodeHelper, pos posrange.PositionRange) (Vector, error) {\n\tvar lastErr error\n\tfor _, lhsSample := range lhs {\n\t\tlf, rf := lhsSample.F, rhs.V\n\t\tvar rh *histogram.FloatHistogram\n\t\tlh := lhsSample.H\n\t\t// lhs always contains the Vector. If the original position was different\n\t\t// swap for calculating the value.\n\t\tif swap {\n\t\t\tlf, rf = rf, lf\n\t\t\tlh, rh = rh, lh\n\t\t}\n\t\tfloat, histogram, keep, err := vectorElemBinop(op, lf, rf, lh, rh, pos)\n\t\tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLWarning) {\n\t\t\tlastErr = err\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Catch cases where the scalar is the LHS in a scalar-vector comparison operation.\n\t\t// We want to always keep the vector element value as the output value, even if it's on the RHS.\n\t\tif op.IsComparisonOperator() && swap {\n\t\t\tfloat = rf\n\t\t\thistogram = rh\n\t\t}\n\t\tif returnBool {\n\t\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\t\tfloat = 1.0\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfloat = 0.0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeep = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\tlhsSample.F = float\n\t\t\tlhsSample.H = histogram\n\t\t\tif changesMetricSchema(op) || returnBool {\n\t\t\t\tif !ev.enableDelayedNameRemoval {\n\t\t\t\t\tlhsSample.Metric = lhsSample.Metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tlhsSample.DropName = true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhsSample)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out, lastErr\n}\n\n// scalarBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Scalars.\nfunc scalarBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs float64) float64 {\n\tswitch op {\n\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\treturn lhs + rhs\n\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\treturn lhs - rhs\n\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\treturn lhs * rhs\n\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\treturn lhs / rhs\n\tcase parser.POW:\n\t\treturn math.Pow(lhs, rhs)\n\tcase parser.MOD:\n\t\treturn math.Mod(lhs, rhs)\n\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs == rhs)\n\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs != rhs)\n\tcase parser.GTR:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs > rhs)\n\tcase parser.LSS:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs < rhs)\n\tcase parser.GTE:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs >= rhs)\n\tcase parser.LTE:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs <= rhs)\n\tcase parser.ATAN2:\n\t\treturn math.Atan2(lhs, rhs)\n\t}\n\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"operator %q not allowed for Scalar operations\", op))\n}\n\n// vectorElemBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Vector elements.\nfunc vectorElemBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs float64, hlhs, hrhs *histogram.FloatHistogram, pos posrange.PositionRange) (float64, *histogram.FloatHistogram, bool, error) {\n\topName := parser.ItemTypeStr[op]\n\tswitch {\n\tcase hlhs == nil && hrhs == nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs + rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs - rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs * rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs / rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.POW:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Pow(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MOD:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Mod(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs == rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs != rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.GTR:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs > rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.LSS:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs < rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.GTE:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs >= rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.LTE:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs <= rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Atan2(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs == nil && hrhs != nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hrhs.Copy().Mul(lhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD, parser.SUB, parser.DIV, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.EQLC, parser.NEQ, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"float\", opName, \"histogram\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs != nil && hrhs == nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs.Copy().Mul(rhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs.Copy().Div(rhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD, parser.SUB, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.EQLC, parser.NEQ, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"histogram\", opName, \"float\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs != nil && hrhs != nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\t\t\tres, counterResetCollision, err := hlhs.Copy().Add(hrhs)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif counterResetCollision {\n\t\t\t\t\terr = annotations.NewHistogramCounterResetCollisionWarning(pos, annotations.HistogramAdd)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, res.Compact(0), true, err\n\t\t\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\t\t\tres, counterResetCollision, err := hlhs.Copy().Sub(hrhs)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif counterResetCollision {\n\t\t\t\t\terr = annotations.NewHistogramCounterResetCollisionWarning(pos, annotations.HistogramSub)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, res.Compact(0), true, err\n\t\t\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\t\t\t// This operation expects that both histograms are compacted.\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs, hlhs.Equals(hrhs), nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\t\t\t// This operation expects that both histograms are compacted.\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs, !hlhs.Equals(hrhs), nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL, parser.DIV, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"histogram\", opName, \"histogram\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"operator %q not allowed for operations between Vectors\", op))\n}\n\ntype groupedAggregation struct {\n\tfloatValue     float64\n\thistogramValue *histogram.FloatHistogram\n\tfloatMean      float64\n\tfloatKahanC    float64 // \"Compensating value\" for Kahan summation.\n\tgroupCount     float64\n\theap           vectorByValueHeap\n\n\t// All bools together for better packing within the struct.\n\tseen                   bool // Was this output groups seen in the input at this timestamp.\n\thasFloat               bool // Has at least 1 float64 sample aggregated.\n\thasHistogram           bool // Has at least 1 histogram sample aggregated.\n\tincompatibleHistograms bool // If true, group has seen mixed exponential and custom buckets, or incompatible custom buckets.\n\tgroupAggrComplete      bool // Used by LIMITK to short-cut series loop when we've reached K elem on every group.\n\tincrementalMean        bool // True after reverting to incremental calculation of the mean value.\n}\n\n// aggregation evaluates sum, avg, count, stdvar, stddev or quantile at one timestep on inputMatrix.\n// These functions produce one output series for each group specified in the expression, with just the labels from `by(...)`.\n// outputMatrix should be already populated with grouping labels; groups is one-to-one with outputMatrix.\n// seriesToResult maps inputMatrix indexes to outputMatrix indexes.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) aggregation(e *parser.AggregateExpr, q float64, inputMatrix, outputMatrix Matrix, seriesToResult []int, groups []groupedAggregation, enh *EvalNodeHelper) annotations.Annotations {\n\top := e.Op\n\tvar annos annotations.Annotations\n\tfor i := range groups {\n\t\tgroups[i].seen = false\n\t}\n\n\tfor si := range inputMatrix {\n\t\tf, h, ok := ev.nextValues(enh.Ts, &inputMatrix[si])\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup := &groups[seriesToResult[si]]\n\t\t// Initialize this group if it's the first time we've seen it.\n\t\tif !group.seen {\n\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\tseen:                   true,\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue:             f,\n\t\t\t\tfloatMean:              f,\n\t\t\t\tincompatibleHistograms: false,\n\t\t\t\tgroupCount:             1,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.AVG, parser.SUM:\n\t\t\t\tif h == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.histogramValue = h.Copy()\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.STDVAR, parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\tcase h != nil:\n\t\t\t\t\t// Ignore histograms for STDVAR and STDDEV.\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tif op == parser.STDVAR {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stdvar\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stddev\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcase math.IsNaN(f), math.IsInf(f, 0):\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = math.NaN()\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = 0\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"quantile\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap = make(vectorByValueHeap, 1)\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = Sample{F: f}\n\t\t\tcase parser.GROUP:\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = 1\n\t\t\tcase parser.MIN, parser.MAX:\n\t\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tif op == parser.MIN {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"min\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"max\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif group.incompatibleHistograms {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.SUM:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\tif group.histogramValue != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t_, _, err := group.histogramValue.Add(h)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise the aggregation contained floats\n\t\t\t\t// previously and will be invalid anyway. No\n\t\t\t\t// point in copying the histogram in that case.\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue, group.floatKahanC = kahanSumInc(f, group.floatValue, group.floatKahanC)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.AVG:\n\t\t\t// For the average calculation of histograms, we use\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation without the help of\n\t\t\t// Kahan summation (but this should change, see\n\t\t\t// https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/14105\n\t\t\t// ). For floats, we improve the accuracy with the help\n\t\t\t// of Kahan summation. For a while, we assumed that\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation combined with Kahan\n\t\t\t// summation (see\n\t\t\t// https://stackoverflow.com/questions/61665473/is-it-beneficial-for-precision-to-calculate-the-incremental-mean-average\n\t\t\t// for inspiration) is generally the preferred solution.\n\t\t\t// However, it then turned out that direct mean\n\t\t\t// calculation (still in combination with Kahan\n\t\t\t// summation) is often more accurate. See discussion in\n\t\t\t// https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/16714\n\t\t\t// . The problem with the direct mean calculation is\n\t\t\t// that it can overflow float64 for inputs on which the\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation works just fine. Our\n\t\t\t// current approach is therefore to use direct mean\n\t\t\t// calculation as long as we do not overflow (or\n\t\t\t// underflow) the running sum. Once the latter would\n\t\t\t// happen, we switch to incremental mean calculation.\n\t\t\t// This seems to work reasonably well, but note that a\n\t\t\t// deeper understanding would be needed to find out if\n\t\t\t// maybe an earlier switch to incremental mean\n\t\t\t// calculation would be better in terms of accuracy.\n\t\t\t// Also, we could apply a number of additional means to\n\t\t\t// improve the accuracy, like processing the values in a\n\t\t\t// particular order. For now, we decided that the\n\t\t\t// current implementation is accurate enough for\n\t\t\t// practical purposes, in particular given that changing\n\t\t\t// the order of summation would be hard, given how the\n\t\t\t// PromQL engine implements aggregations.\n\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\tif group.histogramValue != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tleft := h.Copy().Div(group.groupCount)\n\t\t\t\t\tright := group.histogramValue.Copy().Div(group.groupCount)\n\t\t\t\t\ttoAdd, _, err := left.Sub(right)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t_, _, err = group.histogramValue.Add(toAdd)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise the aggregation contained floats\n\t\t\t\t// previously and will be invalid anyway. No\n\t\t\t\t// point in copying the histogram in that case.\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\tif !group.incrementalMean {\n\t\t\t\t\tnewV, newC := kahanSumInc(f, group.floatValue, group.floatKahanC)\n\t\t\t\t\tif !math.IsInf(newV, 0) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// The sum doesn't overflow, so we propagate it to the\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// group struct and continue with the regular\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// calculation of the mean value.\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue, group.floatKahanC = newV, newC\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t// If we are here, we know that the sum _would_ overflow. So\n\t\t\t\t\t// instead of continue to sum up, we revert to incremental\n\t\t\t\t\t// calculation of the mean value from here on.\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incrementalMean = true\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean = group.floatValue / (group.groupCount - 1)\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatKahanC /= group.groupCount - 1\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tq := (group.groupCount - 1) / group.groupCount\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean, group.floatKahanC = kahanSumInc(\n\t\t\t\t\tf/group.groupCount,\n\t\t\t\t\tq*group.floatMean,\n\t\t\t\t\tq*group.floatKahanC,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.GROUP:\n\t\t\t// Do nothing. Required to avoid the panic in `default:` below.\n\n\t\tcase parser.MAX:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"max\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif group.floatValue < f || math.IsNaN(group.floatValue) {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = f\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.MIN:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"min\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif group.floatValue > f || math.IsNaN(group.floatValue) {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = f\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.COUNT:\n\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDVAR, parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\tif h == nil { // Ignore native histograms.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\t\t\t\tdelta := f - group.floatMean\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean += delta / group.groupCount\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue += delta * (f - group.floatMean)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tif op == parser.STDVAR {\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stdvar\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stddev\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"quantile\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup.heap = append(group.heap, Sample{F: f})\n\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"expected aggregation operator but got %q\", op))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the output matrix from the aggregated groups.\n\tnumSteps := int((ev.endTimestamp-ev.startTimestamp)/ev.interval) + 1\n\n\tfor ri, aggr := range groups {\n\t\tif !aggr.seen {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.AVG:\n\t\t\tif aggr.hasFloat && aggr.hasHistogram {\n\t\t\t\t// We cannot aggregate histogram sample with a float64 sample.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewMixedFloatsHistogramsAggWarning(e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incompatibleHistograms:\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\tcase aggr.hasHistogram:\n\t\t\t\taggr.histogramValue = aggr.histogramValue.Compact(0)\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incrementalMean:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.floatMean + aggr.floatKahanC\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.floatValue/aggr.groupCount + aggr.floatKahanC/aggr.groupCount\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.COUNT:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.groupCount\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDVAR:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue /= aggr.groupCount\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = math.Sqrt(aggr.floatValue / aggr.groupCount)\n\n\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = quantile(q, aggr.heap)\n\n\t\tcase parser.SUM:\n\t\t\tif aggr.hasFloat && aggr.hasHistogram {\n\t\t\t\t// We cannot aggregate histogram sample with a float64 sample.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewMixedFloatsHistogramsAggWarning(e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incompatibleHistograms:\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\tcase aggr.hasHistogram:\n\t\t\t\taggr.histogramValue.Compact(0)\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue += aggr.floatKahanC\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// For other aggregations, we already have the right value.\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tss := &outputMatrix[ri]\n\t\taddToSeries(ss, enh.Ts, aggr.floatValue, aggr.histogramValue, numSteps)\n\t\tss.DropName = inputMatrix[ri].DropName\n\t}\n\n\treturn annos\n}\n\n// aggregationK evaluates topk, bottomk, limitk, or limit_ratio at one timestep on inputMatrix.\n// Output that has the same labels as the input, but just k of them per group.\n// seriesToResult maps inputMatrix indexes to groups indexes.\n// For an instant query, returns a Matrix in descending order for topk or ascending for bottomk, or without any order for limitk / limit_ratio.\n// For a range query, aggregates output in the seriess map.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) aggregationK(e *parser.AggregateExpr, fParam float64, inputMatrix Matrix, seriesToResult []int, groups []groupedAggregation, enh *EvalNodeHelper, seriess map[uint64]Series) (Matrix, annotations.Annotations) {\n\top := e.Op\n\tvar s Sample\n\tvar annos annotations.Annotations\n\t// Used to short-cut the loop for LIMITK if we already collected k elements for every group\n\tgroupsRemaining := len(groups)\n\tfor i := range groups {\n\t\tgroups[i].seen = false\n\t}\n\t// advanceRemainingSeries discards any values at the current timestamp `ts`\n\t// for the remaining input series. In range queries, if these values are not\n\t// consumed now, they will no longer be accessible in the next evaluation step.\n\tadvanceRemainingSeries := func(ts int64, startIdx int) {\n\t\tfor i := startIdx; i < len(inputMatrix); i++ {\n\t\t\t_, _, _ = ev.nextValues(ts, &inputMatrix[i])\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\nseriesLoop:\n\tfor si := range inputMatrix {\n\t\tf, h, ok := ev.nextValues(enh.Ts, &inputMatrix[si])\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\ts = Sample{Metric: inputMatrix[si].Metric, F: f, H: h, DropName: inputMatrix[si].DropName}\n\n\t\tvar k int64\n\t\tvar r float64\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK, parser.BOTTOMK, parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\tk = min(int64(fParam), int64(len(inputMatrix)))\n\t\t\tif k < 1 {\n\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, annos\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase fParam == 0:\n\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, annos\n\t\t\tcase fParam < -1.0:\n\t\t\t\tr = -1.0\n\t\t\tcase fParam > 1.0:\n\t\t\t\tr = 1.0\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\tr = fParam\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup := &groups[seriesToResult[si]]\n\t\t// Initialize this group if it's the first time we've seen it.\n\t\tif !group.seen {\n\t\t\t// LIMIT_RATIO is a special case, as we may not add this very sample to the heap,\n\t\t\t// while we also don't know the final size of it.\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif ratiosampler.AddRatioSample(r, &s) {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 1, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"topk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"bottomk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t// We build a heap of up to k elements, with the smallest element at heap[0].\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase s.H != nil:\n\t\t\t\t// Ignore histogram sample and add info annotation.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"topk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\tcase int64(len(group.heap)) < k:\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\tcase group.heap[0].F < s.F || (math.IsNaN(group.heap[0].F) && !math.IsNaN(s.F)):\n\t\t\t\t// This new element is bigger than the previous smallest element - overwrite that.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\t\tif k > 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Fix(&group.heap, 0) // Maintain the heap invariant.\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t// We build a heap of up to k elements, with the biggest element at heap[0].\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase s.H != nil:\n\t\t\t\t// Ignore histogram sample and add info annotation.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"bottomk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\tcase int64(len(group.heap)) < k:\n\t\t\t\theap.Push((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&group.heap), &s)\n\t\t\tcase group.heap[0].F > s.F || (math.IsNaN(group.heap[0].F) && !math.IsNaN(s.F)):\n\t\t\t\t// This new element is smaller than the previous biggest element - overwrite that.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\t\tif k > 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Fix((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&group.heap), 0) // Maintain the heap invariant.\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\tif int64(len(group.heap)) < k {\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// LIMITK optimization: early break if we've added K elem to _every_ group,\n\t\t\t// especially useful for large timeseries where the user is exploring labels via e.g.\n\t\t\t// limitk(10, my_metric)\n\t\t\tif !group.groupAggrComplete && int64(len(group.heap)) == k {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.groupAggrComplete = true\n\t\t\t\tgroupsRemaining--\n\t\t\t\tif groupsRemaining == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Process other values in the series before breaking the loop in case of range query.\n\t\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak seriesLoop\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tif ratiosampler.AddRatioSample(r, &s) {\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"expected aggregation operator but got %q\", op))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the result from the aggregated groups.\n\tnumSteps := int((ev.endTimestamp-ev.startTimestamp)/ev.interval) + 1\n\tvar mat Matrix\n\tif ev.endTimestamp == ev.startTimestamp {\n\t\tmat = make(Matrix, 0, len(groups))\n\t}\n\n\tadd := func(lbls labels.Labels, f float64, h *histogram.FloatHistogram, dropName bool) {\n\t\t// If this could be an instant query, add directly to the matrix so the result is in consistent order.\n\t\tif ev.endTimestamp == ev.startTimestamp {\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tmat = append(mat, Series{Metric: lbls, Histograms: []HPoint{{T: enh.Ts, H: h}}, DropName: dropName})\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tmat = append(mat, Series{Metric: lbls, Floats: []FPoint{{T: enh.Ts, F: f}}, DropName: dropName})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// Otherwise the results are added into seriess elements.\n\t\t\thash := lbls.Hash()\n\t\t\tss, ok := seriess[hash]\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tss = Series{Metric: lbls, DropName: dropName}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taddToSeries(&ss, enh.Ts, f, h, numSteps)\n\t\t\tseriess[hash] = ss\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, aggr := range groups {\n\t\tif !aggr.seen {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t// The heap keeps the lowest value on top, so reverse it.\n\t\t\tif len(aggr.heap) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse(aggr.heap))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t// The heap keeps the highest value on top, so reverse it.\n\t\t\tif len(aggr.heap) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&aggr.heap)))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMITK, parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn mat, annos\n}\n\n// aggregationCountValues evaluates count_values on vec.\n// Outputs as many series per group as there are values in the input.\nfunc (*evaluator) aggregationCountValues(e *parser.AggregateExpr, grouping []string, valueLabel string, vec Vector, enh *EvalNodeHelper) (Vector, annotations.Annotations) {\n\ttype groupCount struct {\n\t\tlabels labels.Labels\n\t\tcount  int\n\t}\n\tresult := map[uint64]*groupCount{}\n\n\tvar buf []byte\n\tfor _, s := range vec {\n\t\tenh.resetBuilder(s.Metric)\n\t\tif s.H == nil {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(valueLabel, strconv.FormatFloat(s.F, 'f', -1, 64))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(valueLabel, s.H.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric := enh.lb.Labels()\n\n\t\t// Considering the count_values()\n\t\t// operator is less frequently used than other aggregations, we're fine having to\n\t\t// re-compute the grouping key on each step for this case.\n\t\tvar groupingKey uint64\n\t\tgroupingKey, buf = generateGroupingKey(metric, grouping, e.Without, buf)\n\n\t\tgroup, ok := result[groupingKey]\n\t\t// Add a new group if it doesn't exist.\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tresult[groupingKey] = &groupCount{\n\t\t\t\tlabels: generateGroupingLabels(enh, metric, e.Without, grouping),\n\t\t\t\tcount:  1,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup.count++\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the result Vector from the aggregated groups.\n\tfor _, aggr := range result {\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, Sample{\n\t\t\tMetric: aggr.labels,\n\t\t\tF:      float64(aggr.count),\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evaluator) cleanupMetricLabels(v parser.Value) {\n\tif v.Type() == parser.ValueTypeMatrix {\n\t\tmat := v.(Matrix)\n\t\tfor i := range mat {\n\t\t\tif mat[i].DropName {\n\t\t\t\tmat[i].Metric = mat[i].Metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif mat.ContainsSameLabelset() {\n\t\t\tev.errorf(\"vector cannot contain metrics with the same labelset\")\n\t\t}\n\t} else if v.Type() == parser.ValueTypeVector {\n\t\tvec := v.(Vector)\n\t\tfor i := range vec {\n\t\t\tif vec[i].DropName {\n\t\t\t\tvec[i].Metric = vec[i].Metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif vec.ContainsSameLabelset() {\n\t\t\tev.errorf(\"vector cannot contain metrics with the same labelset\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc addToSeries(ss *Series, ts int64, f float64, h *histogram.FloatHistogram, numSteps int) {\n\tif h == nil {\n\t\tif ss.Floats == nil {\n\t\t\tss.Floats = getFPointSlice(numSteps)\n\t\t}\n\t\tss.Floats = append(ss.Floats, FPoint{T: ts, F: f})\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif ss.Histograms == nil {\n\t\tss.Histograms = getHPointSlice(numSteps)\n\t}\n\tss.Histograms = append(ss.Histograms, HPoint{T: ts, H: h})\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) nextValues(ts int64, series *Series) (f float64, h *histogram.FloatHistogram, b bool) {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase len(series.Floats) > 0 && series.Floats[0].T == ts:\n\t\tf = series.Floats[0].F\n\t\tseries.Floats = series.Floats[1:] // Move input vectors forward\n\tcase len(series.Histograms) > 0 && series.Histograms[0].T == ts:\n\t\th = series.Histograms[0].H\n\t\tseries.Histograms = series.Histograms[1:]\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn f, h, false\n\t}\n\treturn f, h, true\n}\n\n// handleAggregationError adds the appropriate annotation based on the aggregation error.\nfunc handleAggregationError(err error, e *parser.AggregateExpr, metricName string, annos *annotations.Annotations) {\n\tpos := e.Expr.PositionRange()\n\tif errors.Is(err, histogram.ErrHistogramsIncompatibleSchema) {\n\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewMixedExponentialCustomHistogramsWarning(metricName, pos))\n\t} else if errors.Is(err, histogram.ErrHistogramsIncompatibleBounds) {\n\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewIncompatibleCustomBucketsHistogramsWarning(metricName, pos))\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleVectorBinopError returns the appropriate annotation based on the vector binary operation error.\nfunc handleVectorBinopError(err error, e *parser.BinaryExpr) annotations.Annotations {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\top := parser.ItemTypeStr[e.Op]\n\tpos := e.PositionRange()\n\tif errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLInfo) || errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLWarning) {\n\t\treturn annotations.New().Add(err)\n\t}\n\t// TODO(NeerajGartia21): Test the exact annotation output once the testing framework can do so.\n\tif errors.Is(err, histogram.ErrHistogramsIncompatibleSchema) || errors.Is(err, histogram.ErrHistogramsIncompatibleBounds) {\n\t\treturn annotations.New().Add(annotations.NewIncompatibleBucketLayoutInBinOpWarning(op, pos))\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// generateGroupingKey builds and returns the grouping key for the given metric and\n// time.Unix(0, 0).UTC()\n\n// LoadedStorage returns storage with generated data using the provided load statements.\n// Non-load statements will cause test errors.\nfunc LoadedStorage(t testutil.T, {\n\trequire.NoError(t, runTest(t, input, engine, newStorage, false))\n}\n\n// testTest allows tests to be run in \"test-the-test\" mode (true for\n// testingMode). newTest() can create the test storage and then return an error,\n\t// and we want to make sure to clean that up to avoid leaking goroutines.\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif test == nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif test.storage != nil {\n\t\t\ttest.storage.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t\tif test.cancelCtx != nil {\n\t\t\ttest.cancelCtx()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, cmd := range test.cmds {\n\t\tif err := test.exec(cmd, engine); err != nil {\n\t\t\t// TODO(fabxc): aggregate command errors, yield diffs for result\n\t\t\t// comparison errors.\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// test is a sequence of read and write commands that are run\n// against a test storage.\ntype test struct {\n\ttestutil.T\n\t// testingMode distinguishes between normal execution and test-execution mode.\n\ttestingMode bool\n\n\tcmds []testCommand\n\n\topen    func(testutil.T) storage.Storage\n\tstorage storage.Storage\n\n\tcontext   context.Context\n\tcancelCtx context.CancelFunc\n}\n\n// newTest returns an initialized empty Test.\nfunc newTest(t testutil.T, input string, testingMode bool, newStorage func(testutil.T) storage.Storage) (*test, error) {\n\ttest := &test{\n\t\tT:           t,\n\t\tcmds:        []testCommand{},\n\t\ttestingMode: testingMode,\n\t\topen:        newStorage,\n\t}\n\terr := test.parse(input)\n\ttest.clear()\n\n\treturn test, err\n}\n\nfunc newTestStorage(t testutil.T) storage.Storage { return teststorage.New(t) }\n\n//go:embed testdata\nvar testsFs embed.FS\n\nfunc raise(line int, format string, v ...any) error {\n\treturn &parser.ParseErr{\n\t\tLineOffset: line,\n\t\tErr:        fmt.Errorf(format, v...),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc parseLoad(lines []string, i int) (int, *loadCmd, error) {\n\tif !patLoad.MatchString(lines[i]) {\n\t\treturn i, nil, raise(i, \"invalid load command. (load[_with_nhcb] <step:duration>)\")\n\t}\n\tparts := patLoad.FindStringSubmatch(lines[i])\n\tvar (\n\t\twithNHCB = parts[1] == \"with_nhcb\"\n\t\tstep     = parts[2]\n\t)\n\tgap, err := model.ParseDuration(step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn i, nil, raise(i, \"invalid step definition %q: %s\", step, err)\n\t}\n\tcmd := newLoadCmd(time.Duration(gap), withNHCB)\n\tfor i+1 < len(lines) {\n\t\ti++\n\t\tdefLine := lines[i]\n\t\tif len(defLine) == 0 {\n\t\t\ti--\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric, vals, err := parseSeries(defLine, i)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tcmd.set(metric, vals...)\n\t}\n\treturn i, cmd, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseSeries(defLine string, line int) (labels.Labels, []parser.SequenceValue, error) {\n\tmetric, vals, err := parser.ParseSeriesDesc(defLine)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tparser.EnrichParseError(err, func(parseErr *parser.ParseErr) {\n\t\t\tparseErr.LineOffset = line\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn labels.Labels{}, nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn metric, vals, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseExpect(defLine string) (expectCmdType, expectCmd, error) {\n\texpectParts := patExpect.FindStringSubmatch(strings.TrimSpace(defLine))\n\texpCmd := expectCmd{}\n\tif expectParts == nil {\n\t\treturn 0, expCmd, errors.New(\"invalid expect statement, must match `expect <type> <match_type>: <string>` format\")\n\t}\n\tvar (\n\t\tmode            = expectParts[1]\n\t\thasOptionalPart = expectParts[2] != \"\"\n\t)\n\texpectType, ok := expectTypeStr[mode]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn 0, expCmd, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid expected error/annotation type %s\", mode)\n\t}\n\tif hasOptionalPart {\n\t\tswitch expectParts[2] {\n\t\tcase \"msg\":\n\t\t\texpCmd.message = strings.TrimSpace(expectParts[3])\n\t\tcase \"regex\":\n\t\t\tpattern := strings.TrimSpace(expectParts[3])\n\t\t\tregex, err := regexp.Compile(pattern)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, expCmd, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid regex %s for %s\", pattern, mode)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\texpCmd.regex = regex\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn 0, expCmd, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid token %s after %s\", expectParts[2], mode)\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\texpCmd.regex = patMatchAny\n\t}\n\treturn expectType, expCmd, nil\n}\n\nfunc validateExpectedCmds(cmd *evalCmd) error {\n\tif len(cmd.expectedCmds[Info]) > 0 && len(cmd.expectedCmds[NoInfo]) > 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid expect lines, info and no_info cannot be used together\")\n\t}\n\tif len(cmd.expectedCmds[Warn]) > 0 && len(cmd.expectedCmds[NoWarn]) > 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid expect lines, warn and no_warn cannot be used together\")\n\t}\n\tif len(cmd.expectedCmds[Fail]) > 1 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid expect lines, multiple expect fail lines are not allowed\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (*test) parseEval(lines []string, i int) (int, *evalCmd, error) {\n\tinstantParts := patEvalInstant.FindStringSubmatch(lines[i])\n\trangeParts := patEvalRange.FindStringSubmatch(lines[i])\n\n\tif instantParts == nil && rangeParts == nil {\n\t\treturn i, nil, raise(i, \"invalid evaluation command. Must be either 'eval[_fail|_warn|_ordered] instant [at <offset:duration>] <query>' or 'eval[_fail|_warn] range from <from> to <to> step <step> <query>'\")\n\t}\n\n\tisInstant := instantParts != nil\n\n\tvar mod string\n\tvar expr string\n\n\tif isInstant {\n\t\tmod = instantParts[1]\n\t\texpr = instantParts[3]\n\t} else {\n\t\tmod = rangeParts[1]\n\t\texpr = rangeParts[5]\n\t}\n\n\t_, err := parser.ParseExpr(expr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tparser.EnrichParseError(err, func(parseErr *parser.ParseErr) {\n\t\t\tparseErr.LineOffset = i\n\t\t\tposOffset := posrange.Pos(strings.Index(lines[i], expr))\n\t\t\tparseErr.PositionRange.Start += posOffset\n\t\t\tparseErr.PositionRange.End += posOffset\n\t\t\tparseErr.Query = lines[i]\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn i, nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tformatErr := func(format string, args ...any) error {\n\t\tcombinedArgs := []any{expr, i + 1}\n\n\t\tcombinedArgs = append(combinedArgs, args...)\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"error in eval %s (line %v): \"+format, combinedArgs...)\n\t}\n\n\tvar cmd *evalCmd\n\n\tif isInstant {\n\t\tat := instantParts[2]\n\t\toffset, err := model.ParseDuration(at)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid timestamp definition %q: %s\", at, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tts := testStartTime.Add(time.Duration(offset))\n\t\tcmd = newInstantEvalCmd(expr, ts, i+1)\n\t} else {\n\t\tfrom := rangeParts[2]\n\t\tto := rangeParts[3]\n\t\tstep := rangeParts[4]\n\n\t\tparsedFrom, err := model.ParseDuration(from)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid start timestamp definition %q: %s\", from, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tparsedTo, err := model.ParseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid end timestamp definition %q: %s\", to, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif parsedTo < parsedFrom {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid test definition, end timestamp (%s) is before start timestamp (%s)\", to, from)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tparsedStep, err := model.ParseDuration(step)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid step definition %q: %s\", step, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcmd = newRangeEvalCmd(expr, testStartTime.Add(time.Duration(parsedFrom)), testStartTime.Add(time.Duration(parsedTo)), time.Duration(parsedStep), i+1)\n\t}\n\n\tswitch mod {\n\tcase \"ordered\":\n\t\t// Ordered results are not supported for range queries, but the regex for range query commands does not allow\n\t\t// asserting an ordered result, so we don't need to do any error checking here.\n\t\tcmd.ordered = true\n\tcase \"fail\":\n\t\tcmd.fail = true\n\tcase \"warn\":\n\t\tcmd.warn = true\n\tcase \"info\":\n\t\tcmd.info = true\n\t}\n\n\tfor j := 1; i+1 < len(lines); j++ {\n\t\ti++\n\t\tdefLine := lines[i]\n\t\tif len(defLine) == 0 {\n\t\t\ti--\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cmd.fail && strings.HasPrefix(defLine, \"expected_fail_message\") {\n\t\t\tcmd.expectedFailMessage = strings.TrimSpace(strings.TrimPrefix(defLine, \"expected_fail_message\"))\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cmd.fail && strings.HasPrefix(defLine, \"expected_fail_regexp\") {\n\t\t\tpattern := strings.TrimSpace(strings.TrimPrefix(defLine, \"expected_fail_regexp\"))\n\t\t\tcmd.expectedFailRegexp, err = regexp.Compile(pattern)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"invalid regexp '%s' for expected_fail_regexp: %w\", pattern, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// This would still allow a metric named 'expect' if it is written as 'expect{}'.\n\t\tif strings.Split(defLine, \" \")[0] == \"expect\" {\n\t\t\tannoType, expectedAnno, err := parseExpect(defLine)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"%w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcmd.expectedCmds[annoType] = append(cmd.expectedCmds[annoType], expectedAnno)\n\t\t\tj--\n\t\t\terr = validateExpectedCmds(cmd)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"%w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif f, err := parseNumber(defLine); err == nil {\n\t\t\tcmd.expect(0, parser.SequenceValue{Value: f})\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric, vals, err := parseSeries(defLine, i)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Currently, we are not expecting any matrices.\n\t\tif len(vals) > 1 && isInstant {\n\t\t\treturn i, nil, formatErr(\"expecting multiple values in instant evaluation not allowed\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tcmd.expectMetric(j, metric, vals...)\n\t}\n\treturn i, cmd, nil\n}\n\n// getLines returns trimmed lines after removing the comments.\nfunc getLines(input string) []string {\n\tlines := strings.Split(input, \"\\n\")\n\tfor i, l := range lines {\n\t\tl = strings.TrimSpace(l)\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(l, \"#\") {\n\t\t\tl = \"\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tlines[i] = l\n\t}\n\treturn lines\n}\n\n// parse the given command sequence and appends it to the test.\nfunc (t *test) parse(input string) error {\n\tlines := getLines(input)\n\tvar err error\n\t// Scan for steps line by line.\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(lines); i++ {\n\t\tl := lines[i]\n\t\tif len(l) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar cmd testCommand\n\n\t\tswitch c := strings.ToLower(patSpace.Split(l, 2)[0]); {\n\t\tcase c == \"clear\":\n\t\t\tcmd = &clearCmd{}\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(c, \"load\"):\n\t\t\ti, cmd, err = parseLoad(lines, i)\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(c, \"eval\"):\n\t\t\ti, cmd, err = t.parseEval(lines, i)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn raise(i, \"invalid command %q\", l)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tt.cmds = append(t.cmds, cmd)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// testCommand is an interface that ensures that only the package internal\n// types can be a valid command for a test.\ntype testCommand interface {\n\ttestCmd()\n}\n\nfunc (*clearCmd) testCmd() {}\nfunc (*loadCmd) testCmd()  {}\nfunc (*evalCmd) testCmd()  {}\n\n// loadCmd is a command that loads sequences of sample values for specific\n// metrics into the storage.\ntype loadCmd struct {\n\tgap       time.Duration\n\tmetrics   map[uint64]labels.Labels\n\tdefs      map[uint64][]promql.Sample\n\texemplars map[uint64][]exemplar.Exemplar\n\twithNHCB  bool\n}\n\nfunc newLoadCmd(gap time.Duration, withNHCB bool) *loadCmd {\n\treturn &loadCmd{\n\t\tgap:       gap,\n\t\tmetrics:   map[uint64]labels.Labels{},\n\t\tdefs:      map[uint64][]promql.Sample{},\n\t\texemplars: map[uint64][]exemplar.Exemplar{},\n\t\twithNHCB:  withNHCB,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (loadCmd) String() string {\n\treturn \"load\"\n}\n\n// set a sequence of sample values for the given metric.\nfunc (cmd *loadCmd) set(m labels.Labels, vals ...parser.SequenceValue) {\n\th := m.Hash()\n\n\tsamples := make([]promql.Sample, 0, len(vals))\n\tts := testStartTime\n\tfor _, v := range vals {\n\t\tif !v.Omitted {\n\t\t\tsamples = append(samples, promql.Sample{\n\t\t\t\tT: ts.UnixNano() / int64(time.Millisecond/time.Nanosecond),\n\t\t\t\tF: v.Value,\n\t\t\t\tH: v.Histogram,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t\tts = ts.Add(cmd.gap)\n\t}\n\tcmd.defs[h] = samples\n\tcmd.metrics[h] = m\n}\n\n// append the defined time series to the storage.\nfunc (cmd *loadCmd) append(a storage.Appender) error {\n\tfor h, smpls := range cmd.defs {\n\t\tm := cmd.metrics[h]\n\n\t\tfor _, s := range smpls {\n\t\t\tif err := appendSample(a, s, m); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif cmd.withNHCB {\n\t\treturn cmd.appendCustomHistogram(a)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\ntype tempHistogramWrapper struct {\n\tmetric        labels.Labels\n\thistogramByTs map[int64]convertnhcb.TempHistogram\n}\n\nfunc newTempHistogramWrapper() tempHistogramWrapper {\n\treturn tempHistogramWrapper{\n\t\thistogramByTs: map[int64]convertnhcb.TempHistogram{},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc processClassicHistogramSeries(m labels.Labels, name string, histogramMap map[uint64]tempHistogramWrapper, smpls []promql.Sample, updateHistogram func(*convertnhcb.TempHistogram, float64)) {\n\tm2 := convertnhcb.GetHistogramMetricBase(m, name)\n\tm2hash := m2.Hash()\n\thistogramWrapper, exists := histogramMap[m2hash]\n\tif !exists {\n\t\thistogramWrapper = newTempHistogramWrapper()\n\t}\n\thistogramWrapper.metric = m2\n\tfor _, s := range smpls {\n\t\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\thistogram, exists := histogramWrapper.histogramByTs[s.T]\n\t\tif !exists {\n\t\t\thistogram = convertnhcb.NewTempHistogram()\n\t\t}\n\t\tupdateHistogram(&histogram, s.F)\n\t\thistogramWrapper.histogramByTs[s.T] = histogram\n\t}\n\thistogramMap[m2hash] = histogramWrapper\n}\n\n// If classic histograms are defined, convert them into native histograms with custom\n// bounds and append the defined time series to the storage.\nfunc (cmd *loadCmd) appendCustomHistogram(a storage.Appender) error {\n\thistogramMap := map[uint64]tempHistogramWrapper{}\n\n\t// Go through all the time series to collate classic histogram data\n\t// and organise them by timestamp.\n\tfor hash, smpls := range cmd.defs {\n\t\tm := cmd.metrics[hash]\n\t\tmName := m.Get(labels.MetricName)\n\t\tsuffixType, name := convertnhcb.GetHistogramMetricBaseName(mName)\n\t\tswitch suffixType {\n\t\tcase convertnhcb.SuffixBucket:\n\t\t\tif !m.Has(labels.BucketLabel) {\n\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"expected bucket label in metric %s\", m))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tle, err := strconv.ParseFloat(m.Get(labels.BucketLabel), 64)\n\t\t\tif err != nil || math.IsNaN(le) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tprocessClassicHistogramSeries(m, name, histogramMap, smpls, func(histogram *convertnhcb.TempHistogram, f float64) {\n\t\t\t\t_ = histogram.SetBucketCount(le, f)\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase convertnhcb.SuffixCount:\n\t\t\tprocessClassicHistogramSeries(m, name, histogramMap, smpls, func(histogram *convertnhcb.TempHistogram, f float64) {\n\t\t\t\t_ = histogram.SetCount(f)\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase convertnhcb.SuffixSum:\n\t\t\tprocessClassicHistogramSeries(m, name, histogramMap, smpls, func(histogram *convertnhcb.TempHistogram, f float64) {\n\t\t\t\t_ = histogram.SetSum(f)\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Convert the collated classic histogram data into native histograms\n\t// with custom bounds and append them to the storage.\n\tfor _, histogramWrapper := range histogramMap {\n\t\tsamples := make([]promql.Sample, 0, len(histogramWrapper.histogramByTs))\n\t\tfor t, histogram := range histogramWrapper.histogramByTs {\n\t\t\th, fh, err := histogram.Convert()\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif fh == nil {\n\t\t\t\tif err := h.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tfh = h.ToFloat(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif err := fh.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\ts := promql.Sample{T: t, H: fh}\n\t\t\tsamples = append(samples, s)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Slice(samples, func(i, j int) bool { return samples[i].T < samples[j].T })\n\t\tfor _, s := range samples {\n\t\t\tif err := appendSample(a, s, histogramWrapper.metric); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc appendSample(a storage.Appender, s promql.Sample, m labels.Labels) error {\n\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\tif _, err := a.AppendHistogram(0, m, s.T, nil, s.H); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif _, err := a.Append(0, m, s.T, s.F); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// evalCmd is a command that evaluates an expression for the given time (range)\n// and expects a specific result.\ntype evalCmd struct {\n\texpr  string\n\tstart time.Time\n\tend   time.Time\n\tstep  time.Duration\n\tline  int\n\n\tisRange                   bool // if false, instant query\n\tfail, warn, ordered, info bool\n\texpectedFailMessage       string\n\texpectedFailRegexp        *regexp.Regexp\n\n\texpectedCmds map[expectCmdType][]expectCmd\n\n\tmetrics      map[uint64]labels.Labels\n\texpectScalar bool\n\texpected     map[uint64]entry\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) isOrdered() bool {\n\treturn ev.ordered || (len(ev.expectedCmds[Ordered]) > 0)\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) isFail() bool {\n\treturn ev.fail || (len(ev.expectedCmds[Fail]) > 0)\n}\n\ntype expectCmdType byte\n\nconst (\n\tOrdered expectCmdType = iota\n\tFail\n\tWarn\n\tNoWarn\n\tInfo\n\tNoInfo\n)\n\nvar expectTypeStr = map[string]expectCmdType{\n\t\"fail\":    Fail,\n\t\"ordered\": Ordered,\n\t\"warn\":    Warn,\n\t\"no_warn\": NoWarn,\n\t\"info\":    Info,\n\t\"no_info\": NoInfo,\n}\n\ntype expectCmd struct {\n\tmessage string\n\tregex   *regexp.Regexp\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) CheckMatch(str string) bool {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn e.message == str\n\t}\n\treturn e.regex.MatchString(str)\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) String() string {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn e.message\n\t}\n\treturn e.regex.String()\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) Type() string {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn \"message\"\n\t}\n\treturn \"pattern\"\n}\n\ntype entry struct {\n\tpos  int\n\tvals []parser.SequenceValue\n}\n\nfunc (e entry) String() string {\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d: %s\", e.pos, e.vals)\n}\n\nfunc newInstantEvalCmd(expr string, start time.Time, line int) *evalCmd {\n\treturn &evalCmd{\n\t\texpr:  expr,\n\t\tstart: start,\n\t\tline:  line,\n\n\t\tmetrics:      map[uint64]labels.Labels{},\n\t\texpected:     map[uint64]entry{},\n\t\texpectedCmds: map[expectCmdType][]expectCmd{},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc newRangeEvalCmd(expr string, start, end time.Time, step time.Duration, line int) *evalCmd {\n\treturn &evalCmd{\n\t\texpr:    expr,\n\t\tstart:   start,\n\t\tend:     end,\n\t\tstep:    step,\n\t\tline:    line,\n\t\tisRange: true,\n\n\t\tmetrics:      map[uint64]labels.Labels{},\n\t\texpected:     map[uint64]entry{},\n\t\texpectedCmds: map[expectCmdType][]expectCmd{},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (*evalCmd) String() string {\n\treturn \"eval\"\n}\n\n// expect adds a sequence of values to the set of expected\n// results for the query.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) expect(pos int, vals ...parser.SequenceValue) {\n\tev.expectScalar = true\n\tev.expected[0] = entry{pos: pos, vals: vals}\n}\n\n// expectMetric adds a new metric with a sequence of values to the set of expected\n// results for the query.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) expectMetric(pos int, m labels.Labels, vals ...parser.SequenceValue) {\n\tev.expectScalar = false\n\n\th := m.Hash()\n\tev.metrics[h] = m\n\tev.expected[h] = entry{pos: pos, vals: vals}\n}\n\n// validateExpectedAnnotationsOfType validates expected messages and regex match actual annotations.\nfunc validateExpectedAnnotationsOfType(expr string, expectedAnnotationsOfType []expectCmd, actualAnnotationsOfType []string, line int, annotationType string, allAnnos annotations.Annotations) error {\n\tif len(expectedAnnotationsOfType) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tif len(actualAnnotationsOfType) == 0 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected %s annotations but none were found for query %q (line %d)\", annotationType, expr, line)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if all expected annotations are found in actual.\n\tfor _, e := range expectedAnnotationsOfType {\n\t\tmatchFound := slices.ContainsFunc(actualAnnotationsOfType, e.CheckMatch)\n\t\tif !matchFound {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(`expected %s annotation matching %s %q but no matching annotation was found for query %q (line %d), found: %v`, annotationType, e.Type(), e.String(), expr, line, allAnnos.AsErrors())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if all actual annotations have a corresponding expected annotation.\n\tfor _, anno := range actualAnnotationsOfType {\n\t\tmatchFound := slices.ContainsFunc(expectedAnnotationsOfType, func(e expectCmd) bool {\n\t\t\treturn e.CheckMatch(anno)\n\t\t})\n\t\tif !matchFound {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected %s annotation %q found for query %s (line %d)\", annotationType, anno, expr, line)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// checkAnnotations asserts if the annotations match the expectations.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) checkAnnotations(expr string, annos annotations.Annotations) error {\n\tcountWarnings, countInfo := annos.CountWarningsAndInfo()\n\tswitch {\n\tcase ev.warn && countWarnings == 0:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected warnings evaluating query %q (line %d) but got none\", expr, ev.line)\n\tcase ev.info && countInfo == 0:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected info annotations evaluating query %q (line %d) but got none\", expr, ev.line)\n\t}\n\n\tvar warnings, infos []string\n\n\tfor _, err := range annos {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLWarning):\n\t\t\twarnings = append(warnings, err.Error())\n\t\tcase errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLInfo):\n\t\t\tinfos = append(infos, err.Error())\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected annotation type, must be either info or warn but got: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif err := validateExpectedAnnotationsOfType(expr, ev.expectedCmds[Warn], warnings, ev.line, \"warn\", annos); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tif err := validateExpectedAnnotationsOfType(expr, ev.expectedCmds[Info], infos, ev.line, \"info\", annos); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tif ev.expectedCmds[NoWarn] != nil && len(warnings) > 0 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected warning annotations evaluating query %q (line %d): %v\", expr, ev.line, annos.AsErrors())\n\t}\n\tif ev.expectedCmds[NoInfo] != nil && len(infos) > 0 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected info annotations evaluating query %q (line %d): %v\", expr, ev.line, annos.AsErrors())\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// compareResult compares the result value with the defined expectation.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) compareResult(result parser.Value) error {\n\tswitch val := result.(type) {\n\tcase promql.Matrix:\n\t\tif ev.isOrdered() {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"expected ordered result, but query returned a matrix\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif ev.expectScalar {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected scalar result, but got matrix %s\", val.String())\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err := assertMatrixSorted(val); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tseen := map[uint64]bool{}\n\t\tfor _, s := range val {\n\t\t\thash := s.Metric.Hash()\n\t\t\tif _, ok := ev.metrics[hash]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected metric %s in result, has %s\", s.Metric, formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tseen[hash] = true\n\t\t\texp := ev.expected[hash]\n\n\t\t\tvar expectedFloats []promql.FPoint\n\t\t\tvar expectedHistograms []promql.HPoint\n\n\t\t\tfor i, e := range exp.vals {\n\t\t\t\tts := ev.start.Add(time.Duration(i) * ev.step)\n\n\t\t\t\tif ts.After(ev.end) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected %v points for %s, but query time range cannot return this many points\", len(exp.vals), ev.metrics[hash])\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tt := ts.UnixNano() / int64(time.Millisecond/time.Nanosecond)\n\n\t\t\t\tif e.Histogram != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\texpectedHistograms = append(expectedHistograms, promql.HPoint{T: t, H: e.Histogram})\n\t\t\t\t} else if !e.Omitted {\n\t\t\t\t\texpectedFloats = append(expectedFloats, promql.FPoint{T: t, F: e.Value})\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif len(expectedFloats) != len(s.Floats) || len(expectedHistograms) != len(s.Histograms) {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected %v float points and %v histogram points for %s, but got %s\", len(expectedFloats), len(expectedHistograms), ev.metrics[hash], formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tfor i, expected := range expectedFloats {\n\t\t\t\tactual := s.Floats[i]\n\n\t\t\t\tif expected.T != actual.T {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected float value at index %v for %s to have timestamp %v, but it had timestamp %v (result has %s)\", i, ev.metrics[hash], expected.T, actual.T, formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif !almost.Equal(actual.F, expected.F, defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected float value at index %v (t=%v) for %s to be %v, but got %v (result has %s)\", i, actual.T, ev.metrics[hash], expected.F, actual.F, formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tfor i, expected := range expectedHistograms {\n\t\t\t\tactual := s.Histograms[i]\n\n\t\t\t\tif expected.T != actual.T {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected histogram value at index %v for %s to have timestamp %v, but it had timestamp %v (result has %s)\", i, ev.metrics[hash], expected.T, actual.T, formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif !compareNativeHistogram(expected.H.Compact(0), actual.H.Compact(0)) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected histogram value at index %v (t=%v) for %s to be %v, but got %v (result has %s)\", i, actual.T, ev.metrics[hash], expected.H.TestExpression(), actual.H.TestExpression(), formatSeriesResult(s))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor hash := range ev.expected {\n\t\t\tif !seen[hash] {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected metric %s not found\", ev.metrics[hash])\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase promql.Vector:\n\t\tif ev.expectScalar {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected scalar result, but got vector %s\", val.String())\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tseen := map[uint64]bool{}\n\t\tfor pos, v := range val {\n\t\t\tfp := v.Metric.Hash()\n\t\t\tif _, ok := ev.metrics[fp]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tif v.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected metric %s in result, has value %s\", v.Metric, HistogramTestExpression(v.H))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected metric %s in result, has value %v\", v.Metric, v.F)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\texp := ev.expected[fp]\n\t\t\tif ev.isOrdered() && exp.pos != pos+1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected metric %s with %v at position %d but was at %d\", v.Metric, exp.vals, exp.pos, pos+1)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\texp0 := exp.vals[0]\n\t\t\texpH := exp0.Histogram\n\t\t\tif expH == nil && v.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected float value %v for %s but got histogram %s\", exp0, v.Metric, HistogramTestExpression(v.H))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif expH != nil && v.H == nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected histogram %s for %s but got float value %v\", HistogramTestExpression(expH), v.Metric, v.F)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif expH != nil && !compareNativeHistogram(expH.Compact(0), v.H.Compact(0)) {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected %v for %s but got %s\", HistogramTestExpression(expH), v.Metric, HistogramTestExpression(v.H))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !almost.Equal(exp0.Value, v.F, defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected %v for %s but got %v\", exp0.Value, v.Metric, v.F)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tseen[fp] = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor fp, expVals := range ev.expected {\n\t\t\tif !seen[fp] {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected metric %s with %v not found\", ev.metrics[fp], expVals)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase promql.Scalar:\n\t\tif !ev.expectScalar {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected vector or matrix result, but got %s\", val.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\texp0 := ev.expected[0].vals[0]\n\t\tif exp0.Histogram != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected histogram %s but got %s\", exp0.Histogram.TestExpression(), val.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !almost.Equal(exp0.Value, val.V, defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected scalar %v but got %v\", exp0.Value, val.V)\n\t\t}\n\n\tdefault:\n\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"promql.Test.compareResult: unexpected result type %T\", result))\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// compareNativeHistogram is helper function to compare two native histograms\n// which can tolerate some differ in the field of float type, such as Count, Sum.\nfunc compareNativeHistogram(exp, cur *histogram.FloatHistogram) bool {\n\tif exp == nil || cur == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif exp.Schema != cur.Schema ||\n\t\t!almost.Equal(exp.Count, cur.Count, defaultEpsilon) ||\n\t\t!almost.Equal(exp.Sum, cur.Sum, defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif exp.UsesCustomBuckets() {\n\t\tif !histogram.FloatBucketsMatch(exp.CustomValues, cur.CustomValues) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif exp.ZeroThreshold != cur.ZeroThreshold ||\n\t\t!almost.Equal(exp.ZeroCount, cur.ZeroCount, defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif !spansMatch(exp.NegativeSpans, cur.NegativeSpans) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif !floatBucketsMatch(exp.NegativeBuckets, cur.NegativeBuckets) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif !spansMatch(exp.PositiveSpans, cur.PositiveSpans) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif !floatBucketsMatch(exp.PositiveBuckets, cur.PositiveBuckets) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc floatBucketsMatch(b1, b2 []float64) bool {\n\tif len(b1) != len(b2) {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tfor i, b := range b1 {\n\t\tif !almost.Equal(b, b2[i], defaultEpsilon) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc spansMatch(s1, s2 []histogram.Span) bool {\n\tif len(s1) == 0 && len(s2) == 0 {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\ts1idx, s2idx := 0, 0\n\tfor {\n\t\tif s1idx >= len(s1) {\n\t\t\treturn allEmptySpans(s2[s2idx:])\n\t\t}\n\t\tif s2idx >= len(s2) {\n\t\t\treturn allEmptySpans(s1[s1idx:])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcurrS1, currS2 := s1[s1idx], s2[s2idx]\n\t\ts1idx++\n\t\ts2idx++\n\t\tif currS1.Length == 0 {\n\t\t\t// This span is zero length, so we add consecutive such spans\n\t\t\t// until we find a non-zero span.\n\t\t\tfor ; s1idx < len(s1) && s1[s1idx].Length == 0; s1idx++ {\n\t\t\t\tcurrS1.Offset += s1[s1idx].Offset\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif s1idx < len(s1) {\n\t\t\t\tcurrS1.Offset += s1[s1idx].Offset\n\t\t\t\tcurrS1.Length = s1[s1idx].Length\n\t\t\t\ts1idx++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif currS2.Length == 0 {\n\t\t\t// This span is zero length, so we add consecutive such spans\n\t\t\t// until we find a non-zero span.\n\t\t\tfor ; s2idx < len(s2) && s2[s2idx].Length == 0; s2idx++ {\n\t\t\t\tcurrS2.Offset += s2[s2idx].Offset\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif s2idx < len(s2) {\n\t\t\t\tcurrS2.Offset += s2[s2idx].Offset\n\t\t\t\tcurrS2.Length = s2[s2idx].Length\n\t\t\t\ts2idx++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif currS1.Length == 0 && currS2.Length == 0 {\n\t\t\t// The last spans of both set are zero length. Previous spans match.\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif currS1.Offset != currS2.Offset || currS1.Length != currS2.Length {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc allEmptySpans(s []histogram.Span) bool {\n\tfor _, ss := range s {\n\t\tif ss.Length > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) checkExpectedFailure(actual error) error {\n\tif ev.expectedFailMessage != \"\" {\n\t\tif ev.expectedFailMessage != actual.Error() {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected error %q evaluating query %q (line %d), but got: %s\", ev.expectedFailMessage, ev.expr, ev.line, actual.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif ev.expectedFailRegexp != nil {\n\t\tif !ev.expectedFailRegexp.MatchString(actual.Error()) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected error matching pattern %q evaluating query %q (line %d), but got: %s\", ev.expectedFailRegexp.String(), ev.expr, ev.line, actual.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\texpFail, exists := ev.expectedCmds[Fail]\n\tif exists && len(expFail) > 0 {\n\t\tif !expFail[0].CheckMatch(actual.Error()) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected error matching %q evaluating query %q (line %d), but got: %s\", expFail[0].String(), ev.expr, ev.line, actual.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// We're not expecting a particular error, or we got the error we expected.\n\t// This test passes.\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc formatSeriesResult(s promql.Series) string {\n\tfloatPlural := \"s\"\n\thistogramPlural := \"s\"\n\n\tif len(s.Floats) == 1 {\n\t\tfloatPlural = \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tif len(s.Histograms) == 1 {\n\t\thistogramPlural = \"\"\n\t}\n\n\thistograms := make([]string, 0, len(s.Histograms))\n\n\tfor _, p := range s.Histograms {\n\t\thistograms = append(histograms, fmt.Sprintf(\"%v @[%v]\", p.H.TestExpression(), p.T))\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%v float point%s %v and %v histogram point%s %v\", len(s.Floats), floatPlural, s.Floats, len(s.Histograms), histogramPlural, histograms)\n}\n\n// HistogramTestExpression returns TestExpression() for the given histogram or \"\" if the histogram is nil.\nfunc HistogramTestExpression(h *histogram.FloatHistogram) string {\n\tif h != nil {\n\t\treturn h.TestExpression()\n\t}\n\treturn \"\"\n}\n\n// clearCmd is a command that wipes the test's storage state.\ntype clearCmd struct{}\n\nfunc (clearCmd) String() string {\n\treturn \"clear\"\n}\n\ntype atModifierTestCase struct {\n\texpr     string\n\tevalTime time.Time\n}\n\nfunc atModifierTestCases(exprStr string, evalTime time.Time) ([]atModifierTestCase, error) {\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(exprStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tts := timestamp.FromTime(evalTime)\n\n\tcontainsNonStepInvariant := false\n\t// Setting the @ timestamp for all selectors to be evalTime.\n\t// If there is a subquery, then the selectors inside it don't get the @ timestamp.\n\t// If any selector already has the @ timestamp set, then it is untouched.\n\tparser.Inspect(expr, func(node parser.Node, path []parser.Node) error {\n\t\tif hasAtModifier(path) {\n\t\t\t// There is a subquery with timestamp in the path,\n\t\t\t// hence don't change any timestamps further.\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch n := node.(type) {\n\t\tcase *parser.VectorSelector:\n\t\t\tif n.Timestamp == nil {\n\t\t\t\tn.Timestamp = makeInt64Pointer(ts)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase *parser.MatrixSelector:\n\t\t\tif vs := n.VectorSelector.(*parser.VectorSelector); vs.Timestamp == nil {\n\t\t\t\tvs.Timestamp = makeInt64Pointer(ts)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase *parser.SubqueryExpr:\n\t\t\tif n.Timestamp == nil {\n\t\t\t\tn.Timestamp = makeInt64Pointer(ts)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase *parser.Call:\n\t\t\t_, ok := promql.AtModifierUnsafeFunctions[n.Func.Name]\n\t\t\tcontainsNonStepInvariant = containsNonStepInvariant || ok\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\n\tif containsNonStepInvariant {\n\t\t// Expression contains a function whose result can vary with evaluation\n\t\t// time, even though its arguments are step invariant: skip it.\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tnewExpr := expr.String() // With all the @ evalTime set.\n\tadditionalEvalTimes := []int64{-10 * ts, 0, ts / 5, ts, 10 * ts}\n\tif ts == 0 {\n\t\tadditionalEvalTimes = []int64{-1000, -ts, 1000}\n\t}\n\ttestCases := make([]atModifierTestCase, 0, len(additionalEvalTimes))\n\tfor _, et := range additionalEvalTimes {\n\t\ttestCases = append(testCases, atModifierTestCase{\n\t\t\texpr:     newExpr,\n\t\t\tevalTime: timestamp.Time(et),\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn testCases, nil\n}\n\nfunc hasAtModifier(path []parser.Node) bool {\n\tfor _, node := range path {\n\t\tif n, ok := node.(*parser.SubqueryExpr); ok string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := &ScrapePoolsDiscovery{ScrapePools: names}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: res, err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targets(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tgetSortedPools := func(targets map[string][]*scrape.Target) ([]string, int) {\n\t\tvar n int\n\t\tpools := make([]string, 0, len(targets))\n\t\tfor p, t := range targets {\n\t\t\tpools = append(pools, p)\n\t\t\tn += len(t)\n\t\t}\n\t\tslices.Sort(pools)\n\t\treturn pools, n\n\t}\n\n\tscrapePool := r.URL.Query().Get(\"scrapePool\")\n\tstate := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"state\"))\n\tshowActive := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"active\"\n\tshowDropped := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"dropped\"\n\tres := &TargetDiscovery{}\n\tbuilder := getSortedPools(targetsActive)\n\t\tres.ActiveTargets = make([]*Target, 0, numTargets)\n\n\t\tfor _, pool := range activePools {\n\t\t\tif scrapePool != \"\" && pool != scrapePool   globalURL.String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError: func() string {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err == nil && lastErrStr == \"\":\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err != matchers {\n\t\tif !m.Matches(lset.Get(m.Name)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targetMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s :=     \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus
